        <p>
         <img alt="nakd bars giveaway" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4028" height="503" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/nakd_bars_giveaway.jpg" width="670"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         I have a really delicious giveaway for you this week!
        </p>
        <p>
         Recently, I was invitedto try out the nakd. whole food bars from
         <a href="http://www.naturalbalancefoods.co.uk" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          Natural Balance foods
         </a>
         and you know, some things are just
         <em>
          <strong>
           too good
          </strong>
         </em>
         not to share!
        </p>
        <p>
         For a chance to
         <strong>
          win an entire mixed box of your own,
         </strong>
         read on and complete the Rafflecopter widget below.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Nakd bars" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4022" height="447" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/nakd_gluten_wheat_dairy_free.jpg" width="670"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         The nakd bars are just that.
        </p>
        <p>
         Naked!
        </p>
        <p>
         They are dairy free, wheat free and gluten fee and have no added sugars or syrups.
        </p>
        <p>
         Nakd bars are made with raw fruit and nuts all smooshed together (they are 100% vegan) and most count as 1 of your 5-a-day!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Nakd whole food bars" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4025" height="447" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Nakd_wholefood_bar.jpg" width="670"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If you have adopted a
         <a href="http://www.naturalbalancefoods.co.uk/community/dietary-needs/should-you-go-on-a-wheat-free-diet/" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          wheat free diet
         </a>
         or lifestyle, these makeagreatsnack  andavailablein so many flavourvarieties!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Nakd caffe mocha" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4023" height="446" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/nakd_caffe_mocha.jpg" width="670"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         Nakd bars have a deliciously dense texture. Moist and chewy, they are good!
        </p>
        <p>
         Having worked my way through them all (
         <em>
          whaaat? you want an honest opinion, right?!
         </em>
         <img alt=":)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
         ) my favourite has to be caffe mocha, with ginger bread coming in a close second.
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh, and if you zap Ginger Bread in the microwave for a few seconds, its ah-mazing.
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Nakd bar flavours" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4017" height="986" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Nakd_bar_flavours.jpg" width="670"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         There werentany flavoursI didnt like and Ive ranked them above in order of my personal preference. The fruity ones weregood, they just werent my faves
         <img alt=":)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         But oh!I noticed Nakd have launched a new Bakewell Tart flavour. Woah, that is one flavour I WILLbe checking out real soon!
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="Nakd bars mixed box" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-4020" height="503" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Nakd_bars_mixed_box.jpg" width="670"/>
        </p>
        <p>
         If like me, youre following a healthy eating plan, dont let hunger strike and catch you off guard.
        </p>
        <p>
         Nakd bars are
         <em>
          perfect
         </em>
         to keep in your car, handbag or desk drawer.
        </p>
        <p>
         Would you like to win a case of your own?
        </p>
        <p>
         <img alt="prize" class="alignnone wp-image-2670 size-full" height="39" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/prize.gif" width="85"/>
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          One (1) mixed case of 18 Nakd bars.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         <img alt="rules" class="alignnone wp-image-2671 size-full" height="39" src="http://onebusywahm.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/01/rules.gif" width="93"/>
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Enter using the Rafflecopter widget below.
         </li>
         <li>
          Open to UK residents only. 18+
         </li>
         <li>
          You can enter in up to 5 ways to boost your chances of winning.
         </li>
         <li>
          The giveaway ends onSunday 12thOctober, 2014 at 11:59 PM (GMT).
         </li>
         <li>
          One (1) prize. One (1) winner receiving 1 mixed case of 18 Nakd bars.
         </li>
         <li>
          Contents of mixed case may vary to those shown above.
         </li>
         <li>
          Giveaway not associated with Twitter or Facebook.
         </li>
         <li>
          No cash alternative.
         </li>
         <li>
          Winner chosen at random via Rafflecopter from valid entries.
         </li>
         <li>
          Winner will be informed by DM. If prize isnt claimed within 72 hoursa new winner may be chosen.
         </li>
         <li>
          One Busy WAHMs decision is final.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         Visit the Rafflecopter widget below to enter.
        </p>
        <p>
         Good luck!
        </p>

            Im vegan so have tried most of these bars and am yet to find one I dont like. I do have a particular pull towards the Mint Cocoa bar though!
           </p>
           <p>
            I highly recommend them to everyone, vegan or not, as they are yum!
           </p>
          </div>

   (function() {
				function addSubmittedClassToFormContainer(e) {
					var form = e.target.form.parentNode;
					var className = 'mc4wp-form-submitted';
					(form.classList) ? form.classList.add(className) : form.className += ' ' + className;

					n.type = 'hidden';
					n.name = h.name;
					n.style.display = 'none';
					n.value = h.value;
					h.parentNode.replaceChild(n,h);
				}

				var forms = document.querySelectorAll('.mc4wp-form');
				for (var i = 0; i &lt; forms.length; i++) {
					(function(f) {

						// make sure honeypot is hidden
						var h = f.querySelector('input[name="_mc4wp_required_but_not_really"]');
						if(h) {
							hideHoneypot(h);
						}

						// add class on submit
						var b = f.querySelector('[type="submit"]');
						if(b.addEventListener) {
							b.addEventListener('click', addSubmittedClassToFormContainer);
						} else {
							b.attachEvent('click', addSubmittedClassToFormContainer);
						}

					})(forms[i]);
				}
			})();
  </script>

  </script>
